*Date: 2018-04-29*

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 9: Austrian Grand Prix
*Date: 2018-07-01*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 14: Italian Grand Prix
*Date: 2018-09-02*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 19: Mexican Grand Prix
*Date: 2018-10-28*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
